add_namespace = amcivwar

### Reed Was President Set up ###
country_event = { # Jack Reed declares revolution against MacArthur
	id = amcivwar.1
	title = amcivwar.1.t
	desc = amcivwar.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_reed
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.1"
		set_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
		USA_release_CSA = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		CSA = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_additional_guns }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 1200
			producer = USA
			}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment_1
			amount = 500
			producer = USA
			}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_tank_equipment
			amount = 20
			producer = USA
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.2
		CSA_initial_events = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		CSA = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_additional_guns }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 1200
			producer = USA
			}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment_1
			amount = 500
			producer = USA
			}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_tank_equipment
			amount = 20
			producer = USA
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.2
		CSA_initial_events = yes
		CSA = {
			change_tag_from = USA
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Old Democrats Breakoff
	id = amcivwar.1001
	title = amcivwar.1001.t
	desc = amcivwar.1001.d
	picture = GFX_USA_murray

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.1001"
		USA_release_COR = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.1001.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		COR = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.2
		COR_initial_events = yes
		hidden_effect = {
		WCC = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				last_election = "1936.11.08"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.1001.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		COR = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.2
		COR = {
			change_tag_from = USA
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		COR_initial_events = yes
		hidden_effect = {
		WCC = {
		set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				last_election = "1936.11.08"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # WCC released
	id = amcivwar.3000
	title = amcivwar.3000.t
	desc = amcivwar.3000.d
	picture = GFX_event_WCC_Denver

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.3000"
		USA_release_WCC = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			WCC = {	
				add_ideas = {
					WCC_Dwight_D_Eisenhower_hog_ade
					WCC_Patrick_J_Hurley_for_ade
					WCC_James_Garesche_Ord_eco_ade
					WCC_Leonard_T_Gerow_sec_ade
					WCC_Omar_Nelson_Bradley_cos
					WCC_Dwight_D_Eisenhower_carm
				}
			}
			WCC_initial_events = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.3000.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		WCC_initial_events = yes
		WCC = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		add_manpower = 15000
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_initial_events = yes
			WCC_initial_events = yes
			if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_reed_was_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.4 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_long_is_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.9 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_murray_is_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.1020 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_garner_is_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.16 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_president_norris }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.19 hours = 8 }
				}
			else_if = {
			limit = { 
			OR = {
			has_global_flag = USA_president_curtis
			has_global_flag = USA_president_landon
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.1300 hours = 8 }
				}
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.5 days = 30 }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_american_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = amcivwar.1313 days = 14 }
			}
			}
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.3000.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		WCC_initial_events = yes
		WCC = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		add_manpower = 15000
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_initial_events = yes
			if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_reed_was_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.4 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_long_is_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.9 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_murray_is_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.1020 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_garner_is_president }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.16 hours = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_president_norris }
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.19 hours = 8 }
				}
			else_if = {
			limit = { 
			OR = {
			has_global_flag = USA_president_curtis
			has_global_flag = USA_president_landon
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.1300 hours = 8 }
				}
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.5 days = 30 }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_american_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = amcivwar.1313 days = 14 }
			}
			}
		WCC = {
			change_tag_from = USA
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # BBR released
	id = amcivwar.3001
	title = amcivwar.3001.t
	desc = amcivwar.3001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_BBR_uprising

	trigger = {
		tag = COR
		COR = {
		OR = {
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		has_government = national_populist
		}
		}
		OR = {
			1167 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = COR }
			1168 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = COR }
			1169 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = COR }
			1170 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = COR }
			1171 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = COR }
		}
		OR = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = ACW_black_nationalist_resistance
			value > 15
			}
		has_completed_focus = COR_black_laws
		has_country_flag = BBR_black_uprising
		}
		NOT = {
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	months = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.3001"
		COR_release_BBR = yes
		set_global_flag = BBR_has_risen_up
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.3001.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		BBR = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		ideology = syndicalist
		popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		ideology = totalist
		popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_stability = 0.2
		add_manpower = 2000
		hidden_effect = {
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = ACW_black_nationalist_resistance
			value = -6
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		COR = {
		country_event = {
		id = amcivwar.3002
		days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.3001.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		BBR = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		ideology = syndicalist
		popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		ideology = totalist
		popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_stability = 0.2
		add_manpower = 2000
		hidden_effect = {
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = ACW_black_nationalist_resistance
			value = -6
			}
		}
		BBR = {
			change_tag_from = COR
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		COR = {
		country_event = {
		id = amcivwar.3002
		days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #War on BBR
	id = amcivwar.3002
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.3002"}
	title = amcivwar.3002.t
	desc = amcivwar.3002.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_gathering_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	show_major = {}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.3002.a
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_manpower = 7000
			declare_war_on = {
			target = BBR
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Demand BBR stand down
	id = amcivwar.3003
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.3003"}
	title = amcivwar.3003.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running
	
	trigger = {
	BBR = {
	exists = yes
	}
    OR = {
        AND = {
	    tag = USA
        NOT = {
            BBR = {
            has_war_with = USA
		    }
	    }
	    TEX = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
        }

        AND = {
	    tag = CAL
		CAL = { 
		NOT = { 
		has_government = national_populist 
		} 
		}
		CAL = { 
		NOT = { 
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		} 
		}
        NOT = {
            BBR = {
            has_war_with = CAL
		    }
	    }
	    TEX = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    USA = {
	        exists = no
		}
        }

        AND = {
	    tag = TEX
		NOT = {
			BBR = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
		}
        NOT = {
            BBR = {
            has_war_with = TEX
		    }
	    }
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    USA = {
	        exists = no
		}
        }
	}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	desc = { ###USA DEMANDS###

	        exists = no
		}

	        exists = no

	        exists = no
		}
        }
    }
	}

	desc = { ###AUS DEMANDS###
	text = amcivwar.3003.d.TEX
	trigger = {
        AND = {
	    tag = TEX
	    OR = {
	        NOT = {
	            BBR = {
	            has_war_with = TEX
			    }
		    }
	    }
	    USA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
        }
    }
	}

	option = { ###The Revolt must rejoin
	name = amcivwar.3003.a
	ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
	}
	BBR = {
	country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.3004
	days = 2
			}
	}
	}

	option = { ###Strike them now
	name = amcivwar.3003.b
	ai_chance = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_ai = no
		}
	}
	declare_war_on = {
	    target = BBR
		type = annex_everything
	}
	}

country_event = { # Reintegration demand
	id = amcivwar.3004
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.3004"}
	title = amcivwar.3004.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	desc = { ###USA demands###
	text = amcivwar.3004.d.USA
	trigger = {
	    TEX = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
		CAL = {
			OR = {
	        		exists = no
			has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
			}
		} 					   
	}
    }
	desc = { ###PSA demands###
	text = amcivwar.3004.d.CAL
	trigger = {
	    USA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    TEX = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
	}
    }
	desc = { ###AUS demands###
	text = amcivwar.3004.d.TEX
	trigger = {
	    USA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    CSA = {
	        exists = no
		}
	    COR = {
	        exists = no
		}
		CAL = {
			OR = {
	        		exists = no
			has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
			}
		}
	}
    }	

	option = {  #Accept
		name = amcivwar.3004.a
		ai_chance = {

			}
		}

	id = amcivwar.4014
	title = amcivwar.4014.t
	desc = amcivwar.4014.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	trigger = {
	tag = CSA
	has_country_flag = CSA_syndicalist_victory
	OR = {
	date > 1938.2.15
	USA = {
	surrender_progress > 0.45
	}
	COR = {
	surrender_progress > 0.45
	}
	}
	CSA = {
	surrender_progress < 0.25
	}
	has_global_flag = AUS_CSA_TREATY
	TEX = {
	exists = yes
	}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 30
	}

		name = amcivwar.4014.a

			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		hidden_effect = {
		TEX = {
		country_event = {
		id = amcivwar.4015 days = 5
			}
		}
		country_event = {
		id = amcivwar.4016 days = 14
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Attack now
		name = amcivwar.4014.b

				target = TEX
				type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
}

country_event = { # Last Men Standing - CSA and AUS
	id = amcivwar.5007
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.5007"}
	title = amcivwar.5007.t
	desc = amcivwar.5007.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Long_Rally

	trigger = {
	tag = TEX
	TEX = {
	exists = yes
	}
	CSA = {
	exists = yes
	}
	NOT = {
	TEX = {
		has_war_with = CSA
		}
	}
	COR = {
	exists = no
	}
	USA = {
	exists = no
	}
	WCC = {
	exists = no
	}
	CAL = {
	exists = no
	}
	has_global_flag = AUS_CSA_TREATY
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 20
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.5007.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		CSA = {
		country_event = { id = amcivwar.5008 hours = 8 }
		}
		}
		add_political_power = -45
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.5007.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_ai = yes
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = AUS_CSA_TREATY
		declare_war_on = {
		target = CSA
		type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = TXS_ACW_TEX }
			TXS = {
				declare_war_on = {
				target = CSA
				type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 40
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.02 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.04 }
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

		}

	id = amcivwar.13

	desc = amcivwar.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest

	trigger = {
	tag = CAL
	OR = {
	has_global_flag = USA_Republicans_Flee
	has_global_flag = USA_Garner_Flees
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 4
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.13.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_global_flag = CAL_confederate_legit_pres
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.13.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAl_peaceo.pngng
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_global_flag = CAL_confederate_legit_pres
		if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = USA_garner_is_president
			}
		create_country_leader = {# John Nance Garner
			name = "John Nance Garner"
			desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_NANCE_GARNER_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_John_Nance_Garner.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = social_conservative_subtype
			traits = { cactus_jack }
			}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = USA_president_landon
		}
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alf Landon"
				desc = "POLITICS_ALF_LANDON_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Alf_Landon_KR.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				traits = { economic_reformer }
			}
			set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = USA_president_curtis
		}
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Charles Curtis"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_CURTIS_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Charles_Curtis_Hat.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"

				traits = { the_great_compromiser }
			}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # CSA wins the civil war
	id = amcivwar.24
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.24"}
	title = amcivwar.24.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_victory_celebration

	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.24.d.noceasefire
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.24.d.ceasefire
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CAN
			has_war_with = MEX
			has_war_with = NEE
			has_war_with = CAL
			has_war_with = BBR
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = COR
			country_exists = WCC
		}
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
			has_global_flag = CAL_not_participating_in_acw
			NOT = {
				country_exists = CAL
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						tag = CSA
						tag = USA
						tag = TEX
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = ACW_survivor
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.24.a
		USA_civil_war_ends = yes
		add_ideas = USA_civil_war_war_aftermath_idea
		add_ideas = USA_civil_war_political_aftermath_idea
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = {
				civilian_economy
				volunteer_only
			}
			USA_demobilize_forces = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = worldnews.42
					days = 1
				}
				country_event = { id = csa.97 days = 115 random = 480 }
				country_event = { id = csa.114 days = 47 }
				country_event = { id = csa.115 days = 31 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = amcivwar.3609.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Purge them
		name = amcivwar.3609.a
		add_political_power = 75
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = -0.07 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = -0.07 }
		add_manpower = -5500
		hidden_effect = {
		CSA = {
			country_event = {
			id = amcivwar.36003
			days = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Purge them
		name = amcivwar.3609.b
		add_political_power = -20
		add_stability = 0.05

		add_manpower = -500
		hidden_effect = {

			id = amcivwar.36003
			days = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = amcivwar.3610.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #We've Won
		name = amcivwar.3610.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_social_patriot_victory
		if = {
			limit = {
				BBR = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
				}
			}
			BBR = {
				country_event = {
					id = bbr.28
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.06 }
		hidden_effect = {
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Socialist American Congress"
				desc = "CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {}
		}
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Socialist American Congress"
				desc = "CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
				traits = { our_right_to_survive }
			}
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Socialist American Congress"
				desc = "CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
				traits = { our_right_to_survive }
			}
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Socialist American Congress"
				desc = "CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"

			}
		}

country_event = { # Hardship of the Revolution
	id = amcivwar.37
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.37"}
	title = amcivwar.37.t
	desc = amcivwar.37.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_scrap_saving

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
		# it's actually winter
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1937.11.1
				date < 1938.2.15
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1938.11.1
				date < 1939.2.15
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.37.a
		add_war_support = -0.03
		add_stability = 0.03
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.37.b
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

	desc = amcivwar.90.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_climbing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		exists = yes
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
			num_of_controlled_states > 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.90.a
		random_list = {
			50 = { add_political_power = 50 }
			25 = { add_political_power = 75 }
			25 = { add_political_power = 100 }
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 750
			producer = CAL
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.90 days = 90 random = 100 }
		}
	}
}

# Reed rebels
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.125
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.125"}
	title = amcivwar.125.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_reed
	
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.125.d.long
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinated_long }
	}
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.125.d.austerity
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_ACW_austerity_rejected }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		USA_release_CSA = yes
		# remove USA cores on AUS territory
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 371
						state = 372
						state = 374
						state = 375
						state = 370
						state = 367
						state = 365
						state = 364
						state = 366
						state = 833
						state = 832
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = USA
				add_claim_by = USA
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.125.a
		CSA = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.2
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_initial_events = yes
			CSA_initial_events = yes
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.127 hours = 8 }
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.128 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.125.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		CSA = {
			set_country_flag = choice_made
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = 0.2
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_initial_events = yes
			CSA_initial_events = yes
			news_event = { id = amcivwar.127 hours = 8 }
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.128 days = 30 }
		}
		CSA = {
			change_tag_from = USA
		}
	}
}

### Foreign Intervention ###
country_event = { # Canadian Intervention
	id = amcivwar.150
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.150"}
	title = amcivwar.150.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.150.d
		trigger = { country_exists = CSA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.150.d.nocsa
		trigger = { NOT = { country_exists = CSA } }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
		OR = {
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = TEX
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
		}
	}

	option = { # We will support a faction
		name = amcivwar.150.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_pass_tariff_act }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = USA_compromise_reached
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_acw_intervention
		#unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_recognize_the_USA
		#unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_recognize_the_PSA
		#unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_recognize_the_AUS
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				country_event = newengland.3
				if = {
					limit = {
						USA = {
							owns_state = 686
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = pri.5 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Activate Defence Plan Two
		name = amcivwar.150.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = USA_compromise_reached
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_taking_land
		if = { # occupy New England
			limit = {
				357 = { is_owned_by = USA }
				} #Maine
			country_event = newengland.1
		}
		if = { # occupy Alaska
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = ALA_chance
				463 = {
					is_owned_by = USA
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.151
				days = 6
			}
		}
		if = { # occupy Puerto Rico
			limit = {
				686 = {
					is_owned_by = USA
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pri.100
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			create_field_marshal = {
				name = "George Pearkes"
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/ALA/Portrait_ALA_George_Pearkes.png"
				traits = { 
					old_guard 
					inflexible_strategist 
				}
				skill = 2
				attack_skill = 1
				defense_skill = 1
				planning_skill = 1
				logistics_skill = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # keep it
		name = amcivwar.153.b
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada Returning land to America ###
	id = amcivwar.156
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.156"}
	title = amcivwar.156.t
	desc = amcivwar.156.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_occupying_USA
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = CAL
			has_war_with = NEE
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = USA
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			is_mainland_america = yes
			NOT = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					country_exists = USA
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_usa
						NOT = {
							country_exists = CAL
							country_exists = CSA
							country_exists = TEX
							country_exists = COR
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_supports_usa
					is_in_faction_with = USA
					USA = {
						is_subject_of = CAN
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					country_exists = CAL
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_psa
						NOT = {
							country_exists = USA
							country_exists = CSA
							country_exists = TEX
							country_exists = COR
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_supports_psa
					is_in_faction_with = CAL
					CAL = {
						is_subject_of = CAN
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					country_exists = TEX
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_aus
						NOT = {
							country_exists = USA
							country_exists = CSA
							country_exists = CAL
							country_exists = COR
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_supports_aus
					is_in_faction_with = TEX
					TEX = {
						is_subject_of = CAN
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = NEE
				OR = {
					NEE = {
						is_subject_of = CAN
					}
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
			USA = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = { # supporting the USA
		name = amcivwar.156.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = USA
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_supports_usa
					NOT = {
						country_exists = CAL
						country_exists = CSA
						country_exists = TEX
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_supports_usa
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				USA = {
					is_subject_of = CAN
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				NOT = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			USA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_returned_land
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = KR_returned_land }
		}
	}
	option = { # Supporting the PSA
		name = amcivwar.156.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = CAL
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_supports_psa
					NOT = {
						country_exists = USA
						country_exists = CSA
						country_exists = TEX
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_supports_psa
				is_in_faction_with = CAL
				CAL = {
					is_subject_of = CAN
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				NOT = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			CAL = {

			}
		}
		CAL = {

	option = { # Giving land to the USA

		trigger = {
			NOT = {

# Peace with Canada?
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.163
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.163"}
	title = amcivwar.163.t
	desc = amcivwar.163.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CSA
			tag = TEX
			tag = CAL
			tag = COR
			tag = HAW
			tag = NEE
			tag = BBR
			tag = WCC
			tag = ALA
			tag = TXS
			}
		has_war_with = CAN
		controls_state = 276 #Southern Ontario
		controls_state = 739 #Ottawa
		NOT = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_controlled_by = CAN
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			owns_state = 276 #Southern Ontario
			owns_state = 739 #Ottawa
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 14
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.163.a
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.164
				days = 3
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = USA_asked_CAN_for_peace
				}
		}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.163.b
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 386
			}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.1641
				days = 3
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = USA_asked_CAN_for_peace_plus
				}
		}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.163.c
		trigger = {
			NEE = {
				exists = yes
				is_ai = yes
				is_subject_of = CAN
				}
			controls_state = 360
			}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.1642
				days = 3
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = USA_asked_CAN_for_peace_plus2
				}
		}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.163.e
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		}
	

}

# PSA accepted
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.167
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.167"}
	title = amcivwar.167.t
	desc = amcivwar.167.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
			name = amcivwar.167.a
			add_political_power = 50
			if = {
				limit = {
					USA = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes	
							has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
							NOT = { has_war_with = CAL }
							}
						}
					}
						
				USA = { country_event = amcivwar.169 }
					}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TEX = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes	
							has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
							NOT = { has_war_with = CAL }
							}
						}
					}
						
				TEX = { country_event = amcivwar.169 }
					}
						
			if = {
				limit = {
					CSA = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes	
							has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
							NOT = { has_war_with = CAL }
							}
						}
					}
						
				CSA = { country_event = amcivwar.169 }
					}
		}
        
}

# Get rid of ACW adjective
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.199
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.199"}
	title = amcivwar.199.t
	desc = amcivwar.199.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = COR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CAL
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = COR
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = USA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = WCC
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CAL
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = CSA
				NOT = {
					country_exists = USA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = COR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = WCC
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CAL
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = TEX
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = COR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = WCC
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = USA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CAL
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = CAL
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = COR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = WCC
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = USA
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.199.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = USA_ACW
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			CSA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = CSA_ACW
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			COR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = COR_ACW
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			TEX = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = TEX_ACW
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			CAL = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = CAL_ACW
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


### Rocky Mountain Ceasefire Events ###

# When there's only PSA and one other faction left
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.200
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.200"}
	title = amcivwar.200.t
	desc = amcivwar.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				NOT = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = CSA
				NOT = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = USA
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = TEX
				NOT = {
					country_exists = USA
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		has_war_with = CAL
		surrender_progress < 0.50
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			is_in_faction = no
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
			any_enemy_country = {
				NOT = {
					tag = CAL
					is_subject_of = CAL
				}
			}
		}
		CAL = {
			exists = yes
			surrender_progress < 0.50
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.200.a #Let us propose the ceasefire
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		ROOT = {
			save_event_target_as = survivor
		}
		CAL = {
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.201
				days = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.202
				days = 5
			}
			CAL = {
				country_event = {
					id = amcivwar.202
					days = 5
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.203
				days = 7
			}
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.204
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.200.b #No, there's no point
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				tag = CSA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				tag = USA
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}

# Ceasefire Talks Fall Apart
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.203
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.203"}
	title = amcivwar.203.t
	desc = amcivwar.203.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			tag = CAL
			tag = event_target:survivor
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		CAL = {
			has_war_with = event_target:survivor
		}

		NOT = {
			AND = {
				event_target:survivor = {
					has_country_flag = ACW_ceasefire_agreed
				}
				CAL = {
					has_country_flag = ACW_ceasefire_agreed
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.203.a
		clr_country_flag = ACW_ceasefire_agreed
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = event_target:survivor
				modifier = small_decrease
			}
			else = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = CAL
					modifier = small_decrease
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = amcivwar.204.t
	desc = amcivwar.204.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		CAL = {
			has_war_with = event_target:survivor
		}

		event_target:survivor = {
			has_country_flag = ACW_ceasefire_agreed
		}
		CAL = {
			has_country_flag = ACW_ceasefire_agreed
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		# Montana or Wyoming controlled by CAL - both go to CAL
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					388 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Montana
					381 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Wyoming
				}
			}
			388 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1157 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			381 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1164 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# North or South Dakota controlled by CAL - both go to CAL if Montana is
		if = {
			limit = {
				388 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Montana
				OR = {
					389 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #North Dakota
					390 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #South Dakota
				}
			}
			389 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			390 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Minnesota controlled by CAL - goes to CAL if North Dakota is
		if = {
			limit = {
				389 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #North Dakota
				391 = {
					is_controlled_by = CAL
					} #Minnesota
			}
			391 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1173 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Colorado or New Mexico controlled by CAL - both go to CAL
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					382 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Colorado
					376 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #New Mexico
				}
			}
			382 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1150 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1174 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			376 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1161 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1096 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1175 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Northern or Southern Texas controlled by CAL - all of Texas goes to CAL if New Mexico is
		if = {
			limit = {
				376 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #New Mexico
				OR = {
					375 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Northern Texas
					833 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Southern Texas
				}
			}
			375 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			832 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			833 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1166 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Kansas Controlled by CAL - goes to CAL if Colorado is
		if = {
			limit = {
				382 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Colorado
				383 = {
					is_controlled_by = CAL
					} #Kansas
			}
			383 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Both Kansas and Northern Texas going to CAL - so is Oklahoma
		if = {
			limit = {
				383 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Kansas
				375 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Northern Texas
			}
			374 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
				} #Oklahoma
		}
		# Louisiana or Arkansas controlled by CAL - both go to CAL if Oklahoma and Northern Texas are
		if = {
			limit = {
				374 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Oklahoma
				375 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Northern Texas
				OR = {
					371 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Louisiana
					372 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Arkansas
				}
			}
			371 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			372 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1156 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Nebraska goes to CAL if both South Dakota/Kansas are or two bordering states are
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						390 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #South Dakota
						381 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #Wyoming
						384 = {
							is_controlled_by = CAL
							} #Nebraska
					}
					AND = {
						383 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #Kansas
						382 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #Colorado
						384 = {
							is_controlled_by = CAL
							} #Nebraska
					}
					AND = {
						390 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #South Dakota
						383 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #Kansas
					}
				}
			}
			384 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Missouri and Iowa go to CAL if surrounding states are
		if = {
			limit = {
				384 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Nebraska
				383 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					} #Kansas
				OR = {
					373 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Missouri
					392 = {
						is_controlled_by = CAL
						} #Iowa
					AND = {
						391 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #Minnesota
						372 = {
							has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
							} #Arkansas
					}
				}
			}
			373 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			1163 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
			392 = {
				set_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}
		# Not Louisiana if it's AUS
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:survivor = {
					tag = TEX
				}
				371 = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
				}
			}
			371 = {
				clr_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
			}
		}

		# Name the Ceasefire
		if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					391 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					392 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					373 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					372 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					371 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
				}
			}
			CAL = {
				set_country_flag = CAL_miss_ceasefire_name
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					375 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					383 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					384 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
					390 = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					}
				}
			}
			CAL = {
				set_country_flag = CAL_plains_ceasefire_name
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAL = {
				set_country_flag = CAL_rocky_ceasefire_name
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.204.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		CAL = {
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = {
					region = 118 #West Coast
					region = 185 #North West
					state = 463 #Alaska
					state = 380 #Utah
					state = 377 #Arizona
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
				}
			}
			CAL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CAL = {
				country_event = {
					id = amcivwar.205
					hours = 8
				}
			}
			news_event = {
				id = amcivwar.206
				hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	trigger = { 
	NOT = { tag = CAL } 
	has_global_flag = WCC_annexation
	CAL = {
	exists = yes
	}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 60
	}

	option = { #Damn
		name = amcivwar.2042.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CAL
			type = annex_everything
		}

			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TXS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

# PSA informed
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.205
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.205"}
	title = amcivwar.205.t
	desc = amcivwar.205.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.205.a
		set_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
		add_stability = 0.05

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				is_mainland_america = yes
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_ceasefire_state
					region = 118 #West Coast
					region = 185 #North West
					state = 463 #Alaska
					state = 380 #Utah
					state = 377 #Arizona
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = FROM
						is_core_of = FROM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
					remove_claim_by = FROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = FROM
					}
					remove_core_of = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = CAL
							is_core_of = CAL
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = CAL
						}
						remove_claim_by = CAL
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = CAL
						}
						remove_core_of = CAL
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### America's colonies in the Philippines and Liberia ###
country_event = { # America in Chaos
	id = amcivwar.212
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.212"}
	title = amcivwar.212.t
	desc = amcivwar.212.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = "LIB"
		is_subject_of = USA
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Lapdogs no longer - We can protect ourselves!
		name = amcivwar.212.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_idea = LIB_firestone_bailout
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = LIB_bailout_usa_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = LIB_bailout_usa_2
				add_idea = LIB_bailout_usa
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = LIB_no_longer_puppet
		overlord = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = LIB
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = LIB_goes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = MAF
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				MAF = {
					country_event = {
						id = amcivwar.222
						days = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = LIB_Liberian_Frontier_Force
					}
					swap_ideas = {
                    remove_idea = LIB_Liberian_Frontier_Force
                    add_idea = LIB_Liberian_Frontier_Force2
                	}
				}
			}
		}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes
	}
	option = { # We aren't traitors - Stay loyal to the Americans
		name = amcivwar.212.e

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_idea = LIB_bailout_usa
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = LIB_stand
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_liberia_rally
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = LIB_IND
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
}

country_event = { # The German-Afrikaans attack
	id = amcivwar.225
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.225"}
	title = amcivwar.225.t
	desc = amcivwar.225.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.225.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_liberia_rally
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = LIB_WAR_GER
		}
	}
}

##### the Philippines events ####
country_event = { # America in Chaos
	id = amcivwar.226
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.226"}
	title = amcivwar.226.t
	desc = amcivwar.226.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = PHI
		is_subject_of = USA
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.226.a
		clr_country_flag = puppet_of_usa
		overlord = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PHI
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_global_flag = PHI_FREEDOM
		separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.229
				days = 14
			}
			country_event = {
				id = amcivwar.227
				days = 17
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Philippines Seizing equipment
	id = amcivwar.227
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.227"}
	title = amcivwar.227.t
	desc = amcivwar.227.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = PHI
		has_global_flag = PHI_FREEDOM
		country_exists = USA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.227.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 66
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = PHI_SIZE_EQUIP
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 2500
			producer = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.227.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 34
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = PHI_NO_EQUIP
		}
	}
}

### Pre-War Events
country_event = { # New England Riots
	id = amcivwar.300
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.300"}
	title = amcivwar.300.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots
	
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.300.d.assass
		trigger = { USA = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinated_reed } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.300.d.peace
		trigger = { USA = { has_country_flag = USA_ACW_compromise_rejected } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = amcivwar.300.d
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_ACW_compromise_rejected
					has_country_flag = USA_assassinated_reed
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	show_major = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CSA
			tag = COR
			tag = TEX
			tag = CAL
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag }
		OR = {
			357 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			358 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			359 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			934 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			933 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			796 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			932 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			931 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
			935 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.300.a
		trigger = { tag = USA }
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.300.b
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = USA } }
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
}

country_event = { # Bounce event for Minnesota
	id = amcivwar.301
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.301"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag }
		391 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
	}

	option = {
		name = GO_CSA
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				USA = { has_country_flag = USA_minnesota_order }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				USA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_minnesota_order } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength > 2 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength > 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength > 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength > 5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength > 6 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength > 7 } }
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = amcivwar.320
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = STAY_USA
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength < 2 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength < 1 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = { check_variable = { SPA_strength < 0 } }
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = amcivwar.321
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Nevada flips to PSA
	id = amcivwar.310
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.310"}
	title = amcivwar.310.t
	desc = amcivwar.310.d
	picture = GFX_CAL_legislature

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CSA
			tag = TEX
			tag = CAL
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CAL
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag }
		379 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
		CAL = { is_ai = yes }
		NOT = {
			CSA = { is_ai = no }
			TEX = { is_ai = no }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CAL = { transfer_state = 379 }
			379 = {
				remove_claim_by = CAL
				add_core_of = CAL
				remove_core_of = USA
				add_claim_by = USA
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.310.a
		trigger = { tag = CAL }
	}
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.310.b
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = CAL } }
	}
}

# Getting cores on controlled lands
country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.314
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.314"}
	title = amcivwar.314.t
	desc = amcivwar.314.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_american_brigade

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CSA
			tag = TEX
			tag = CAL
			tag = COR
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
		any_of_scopes = {
			array = controlled_states
			THIS = {
				OR = {
					has_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT
					state = 379 #Nevada
					state = 832 #Trans-Pecos
					AND = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								tag = USA
								tag = CAL
							}
						}
						OR = {
							state = 376 #New Mexico
							state = 377 #Arizona
							state = 380 #Utah
							state = 387 #Idaho
							state = 388 #Montana
							state = 389 #North Dakota
							state = 390 #South Dakota
						}
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								tag = USA
							}
						}
						OR = {
							state = 930 #Delaware
							state = 933 #Vermont
							state = 934 #New Hampshire
							state = 935 #Rhode Island
						}
					}
				}
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				ROOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV }
				any_neighbor_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			tag = CSA
			USA = { has_global_flag = USA_reed_was_president }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			tag = TEX
			USA = { has_global_flag = USA_long_is_president }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			tag = CAL
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			tag = USA
			has_elected_government = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { tag = USA }
			USA = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_ACW_compromise_rejected
					has_country_flag = USA_ACW_austerity_rejected
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT
						state = 379 #Nevada
						state = 832 #Trans-Pecos
						AND = {
							ROOT = {
								NOT = {
									tag = USA
									tag = CAL
								}
							}
							OR = {
								state = 376 #New Mexico
								state = 377 #Arizona
								state = 380 #Utah
								state = 387 #Idaho
								state = 388 #Montana
								state = 389 #North Dakota
								state = 390 #South Dakota
							}
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = {
								NOT = {
									tag = USA
								}
							}
							OR = {
								state = 930 #Delaware
								state = 933 #Vermont
								state = 934 #New Hampshire
								state = 935 #Rhode Island
							}
						}
					}
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					ROOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV }
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = restored_core
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.314.a
		event_target:restored_core = {
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
	}
}

### Surrender Checks ###
country_event = { # USA Surrenders
	id = amcivwar.600
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.600"}
	title = amcivwar.600.t
	desc = amcivwar.600.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
		OR = {
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = COR
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = CAL
		}
		
		#check number of controlled states in the continental USA
		set_temp_variable = { global.num = 0 }
		all_of = {
			array = controlled_states
			var:v = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_mainland_america = yes }
					add_to_temp_variable = { global.num = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		OR = {
			check_variable = { global.num < 2 } #down to last state
			surrender_progress > 0.85
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				controls_state = 361 #Maryland
				surrender_progress > 0.60
				check_variable = { global.num < 4 } #controls 3 or less states
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						controls_state = 382 #Colorado
						382 = { is_core_of = USA }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 797 #San Francisco
						797 = { is_core_of = USA }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 798 #Los Angeles
						798 = { is_core_of = USA }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 375 #Northern Texas
						375 = { is_core_of = USA }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 395 #Illinois
						395 = { is_core_of = USA }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 358 #New York City
						358 = { is_core_of = USA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					361 = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				361 = {
					controller = {
						save_event_target_as = annex_to
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					382 = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				382 = {
					controller = {
						save_event_target_as = annex_to
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = CSA
							tag = COR
							tag = TEX
							tag = CAL
							tag = USA
						}
					}
				}
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = CSA
							tag = COR
							tag = TEX
							tag = CAL
							tag = USA
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = annex_to
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						exists = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = CSA
							tag = COR
							tag = TEX
							tag = CAL
							tag = USA
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = annex_to
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = last_state
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.600.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = amcivwar_idea
			}
			remove_ideas = amcivwar_idea
		}
		ACW_surrender_effect = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = amcivwar_surrender_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = amcviwar_ready_to_surrender
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:annex_to = {
				news_event = amcivwar.607
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			remove_ideas = amcivwar_idea
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = amcivwar_surrender_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = amcviwar_ready_to_surrender
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:annex_to = {
				news_event = amcivwar.610
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # WCC Surrenders
	id = amcivwar.6004
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.6004"}
	title = amcivwar.600.t
	desc = amcivwar.600.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = WCC
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
		OR = {
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = COR
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = CAL
		}
		
		#check number of controlled states in the continental USA
		set_temp_variable = { global.num = 0 }
		all_of = {
			array = controlled_states
			var:v = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_mainland_america = yes }
					add_to_temp_variable = { global.num = 1 }
				}
			}
		}		
		
		OR = {
			check_variable = { global.num < 2 } #down to last state
			surrender_progress > 0.85
			AND = {
				controls_state = 382 # Colorado
				surrender_progress > 0.80
				check_variable = { global.num < 4 } #controls 3 or less states
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						controls_state = 361 #Washington
						361 = { is_core_of = WCC }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 797 #San Francisco
						797 = { is_core_of = WCC }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 798 #Los Angeles
						798 = { is_core_of = WCC }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 375 #Northern Texas
						375 = { is_core_of = WCC }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 395 #Illinois
						395 = { is_core_of = WCC }
					}
					AND = {
						controls_state = 358 #New York City
						358 = { is_core_of = WCC }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					382 = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				382 = {
					controller = {
						save_event_target_as = annex_to
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					1112 = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				1112 = {
					controller = {
						save_event_target_as = annex_to
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = CSA
							tag = COR
							tag = TEX
							tag = CAL
							tag = USA
						}
					}
				}
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = CSA
							tag = COR
							tag = TEX
							tag = CAL
							tag = USA
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = annex_to
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						exists = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = CSA
							tag = COR
							tag = TEX
							tag = CAL
							tag = USA
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = annex_to
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = last_state
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.600.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = amcivwar_idea
			}
			remove_ideas = amcivwar_idea
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = amcivwar_surrender_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = amcviwar_ready_to_surrender
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:annex_to = {
				news_event = amcivwar.609
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Cleanup event
	id = amcivwar.606
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.606"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

					country_exists = USA

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		NOT = {
			tag = USA
		}

	}

	id = amcivwar.615
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.615"}

	desc = amcivwar.615.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.615.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_units_recalled
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Emergency National Guard"
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 0
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 1
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 2
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 3
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 1
						y = 0
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 1
						y = 1
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 1
						y = 2
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 2
						y = 0
					}
					infantry = {
						x = 2
						y = 1
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
					OR = {
						state = 261 #Ohio
						state = 358 #New York
						state = 360 #Pennsylvania
						state = 361 #Maryland
						state = 365 #Georgia
						state = 367 #Alabama
						state = 370 #Mississippi
						state = 373 #Missouri
						state = 375 #Texas
						state = 378 #California
						state = 382 #Colorado
						state = 383 #Kansas
						state = 386 #Washington
						state = 392 #Iowa
						state = 393 #Michigan
						state = 395 #Illinois
						state = 396 #Indiana
						state = 798 #Los Angeles
						state = 797 #San Francisco
						state = 932 #Massachusetts
					}
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Emergency Guard Unit\" division_template = \"Emergency National Guard\"  start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = amcivwar.616
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.616"}
	title = amcivwar.616.t
	desc = amcivwar.616.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_american_brigade

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CAL
			tag = TEX
			tag = CSA
		}
		has_country_flag = ACW_attacked_during_recovery
		has_template = "Emergency National Guard"
		has_war = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = ACW_attacked_during_recovery
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.616.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_template = "Emergency National Guard"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Emergency National Guard"
			}
		}
	}
}

			exists = yes
		}
		tag = TEX
	}

	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.617.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		set_country_flag = TEX_no_catholic
	}

		name = amcivwar.617.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TEX_post_civil_war
					option = TEX_POST_CIVIL_WAR_CATHOLIC_AMERICA
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TEX_allowed_catholic
		add_manpower = 500
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 2500 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 5500 }
	}

			  value < 15
			}
		OR = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = ACW_black_legion_resistance
			value > 10
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = ACW_black_legion_resistance
			value = 10
		}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_idea = ACW_black_legion_resistance_2 
			has_idea = ACW_black_legion_resistance_3 
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 15
	}
	
	option = { # Level 2 resistance
		name = amcivwar.620.a
		if = {
		 limit = { has_idea = ACW_black_legion_resistance_1 }
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = ACW_black_legion_resistance_1
		add_idea = ACW_black_legion_resistance_2
			}
		}
		else = {
		add_ideas = ACW_black_legion_resistance_2
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Panama Garrison
	id = amcivwar.1312
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event amcivwar.1312"}
	title = amcivwar.1312.t
	desc = amcivwar.1312.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers1

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = BBR
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "CAR Militia" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "CAR Militia" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "CAR Motorized Division" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "CAR Motorized Division" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "CAR Garrison" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "CAR Garrison" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "CAR Infantry Division" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "CAR Infantry Division" }
			}
	}

	option = { # Flavor
		name = amcivwar.1312.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_bbr_unit_tooltip
	}
}
